tRule▷missing◁$ፐ = '.--.' ;
tRule▷missing◁([.-])' '[$] → $1;
tRule▷missing◁([:Lo:])([:Zs:]+)([:Lo:]) → | $1⁄⁂⁄$2$3 ; # ⁄⁂⁄ is assumed to be a sufficiently weird enough sequence that won't naturally appear in any normal content
tRule▷missing◁0 ↔ '----- ' ;
tRule▷missing◁1 ↔ '.---- ' ;
tRule▷missing◁2 ↔ '..--- ' ;
tRule▷missing◁3 ↔ '...-- ' ;

tRule▷missing◁8 ↔ '---.. ' ;
tRule▷missing◁9 ↔ '----. ' ;
tRule▷missing◁:: ([.- ]) ;
tRule▷missing◁:: [[:Zs:]0-9!\?\+/@()\[\]_:;,\.'"$=\-[:Ethiopic:]] ;
tRule▷missing◁::Null;

tRule▷missing◁\" ↔ '.-..-. ' ;

tRule▷missing◁\' ↔ '.----. ' ;
tRule▷missing◁\( ↔ '-.--. ' ;

tRule▷missing◁\= → '-...- ' ;
